Śrīmad-Bhāgavatam

Canto 10: The Summum Bonum

CHAPTER THIRTEEN

The Stealing of the Boys and Calves by Brahmā

This chapter describes Lord Brahmā’s attempt to take away the calves and cowherd boys, and it also describes the bewilderment of Lord Brahmā and finally the clearance of his illusion.

Although the incident concerning Aghāsura had been performed one year before, when the cowherd boys were five years old, when they were six years old they said, “It happened today.” What happened was this. After killing Aghāsura, Kṛṣṇa, along with His associates the cowherd boys, went for a picnic within the forest. The calves, being allured by green grasses, gradually went far away, and therefore Kṛṣṇa’s associates became a little agitated and wanted to bring back the calves. Kṛṣṇa, however, encouraged the boys by saying, “You take your tiffin without being agitated. I shall go find the calves.” And thus the Lord departed. Then, just to examine the potency of Kṛṣṇa, Lord Brahmā took away all the calves and cowherd boys and kept them in a secluded place.

When Kṛṣṇa was unable to find the calves and boys, He could understand that this was a trick performed by Brahmā. Then the Supreme Personality of Godhead, the cause of all causes, in order to please Lord Brahmā, as well as His own associates and their mothers, expanded Himself to become the calves and boys, exactly as they were before. In this way, He discovered another pastime. A special feature of this pastime was that the mothers of the cowherd boys thus became more attached to their respective sons, and the cows became more attached to their calves. After nearly a year, Baladeva observed that all the cowherd boys and calves were expansions of Kṛṣṇa. Thus He inquired from Kṛṣṇa and was informed of what had happened.

When one full year had passed, Brahmā returned and saw that Kṛṣṇa was still engaged as usual with His friends and the calves and cows. Then Kṛṣṇa exhibited all the calves and cowherd boys as four-armed forms of Nārāyaṇa. Brahmā could then understand Kṛṣṇa’s potency, and he was astonished by the pastimes of Kṛṣṇa, his worshipable Lord. Kṛṣṇa, however, bestowed His causeless mercy upon Brahmā and released him from illusion. Thus Brahmā began to offer prayers to glorify the Supreme Personality of Godhead.

Synonyms

śrī-śukaḥ uvāca — Śukadeva Gosvāmī said; sādhu pṛṣṭam — I have been very much honored by your inquiry; mahā-bhāga — you are a greatly fortunate personality; tvayā — by you; bhāgavata-uttama — O best of devotees; yat — because; nūtanayasi — you are making newer and newer; īśasya — of the Supreme Personality of Godhead; śṛṇvan api — although you are continuously hearing; kathām — the pastimes; muhuḥ — again and again.

ศฺรี - ศรี-ศุกห์ - ศุกะห์ อุวาจ - อุวาจะ — Śukadeva Gosvāmī said; สาธุ - สาธุ ปฺฤษฺฏมฺ - ปฤษฏัม — I have been very much honored by your inquiry; มหา - มะหา-ภาค - ภาคะ — you are a greatly fortunate personality; ตฺวยา - ตวะยา — by you; ภาควต - ภาคะวะตะ-อุตฺตม - อุตตะมะ — O best of devotees; ยตฺ - ยัต — because; นูตนยสิ - นูตะนะยะสิ — you are making newer and newer; อีศสฺย - อีศัสยะ — of the Supreme Personality of Godhead; ศฺฤณฺวนฺ - ศฤณวัน อปิ - อะปิ — although you are continuously hearing; กถามฺ - กะถาม — the pastimes; มุหุห์ - มุหุห์ — again and again.

Translation

Śrīla Śukadeva Gosvāmī said: O best of devotees, most fortunate Parīkṣit, you have inquired very nicely, for although constantly hearing the pastimes of the Lord, you are perceiving His activities to be newer and newer.

Purport

Unless one is very advanced in Kṛṣṇa consciousness, one cannot stick to hearing the pastimes of the Lord constantly. Nityaṁ nava-navāya-mānam: - นิตฺยํ นว-นวาย-มานมฺ: - นิตยัง นะวะ-นะวายะ-มานัม: even though advanced devotees hear continually about the Lord for years, they still feel that these topics are coming to them as newer and fresher. Therefore such devotees cannot give up hearing of the pastimes of Lord Kṛṣṇa. Premāñjana-cchurita-bhakti-vilocanena santaḥ sadaiva hṛdayeṣu vilokayanti. - เปฺรมาญฺชน-จฺฉุริต-ภกฺติ-วิโลจเนน สนฺตห์ สไทว หฺฤทเยษุ วิโลกยนฺติฯ - ปเรมาญชะนะ-จฉุริตะ-ภักติ-วิโลจะเนนะ สันตะห์ สะไทวะ หฤทะเยษุ วิโลกะยันติฯ The word santaḥ - สนฺตห์ - สันตะห์ is used to refer to persons who have developed love for Kṛṣṇa. Yaṁ śyāmasundaram acintya-guṇa-svarūpaṁ govindam ādi-puruṣaṁ tam ahaṁ bhajāmi - ยํ ศฺยามสุนฺทรมฺ อจินฺตฺย-คุณ-สฺวรูปํ โควินฺทมฺ อาทิ-ปุรุษํ ตมฺ อหํ ภชามิ - ยัง ศยามะสุนทะรัม อะจินตยะ-คุณะ-สวะรูปัง โควินทัม อาทิ-ปุรุษัง ตัม อะหัง ภะชามิ (Brahma-saṁhitā - พฺรหฺม-สํหิตา - พรัหมะ-สังหิตา 5.38). Parīkṣit Mahārāja, therefore, is addressed as bhāgavatottama, - ภาควโตตฺตม, - ภาคะวะโตตตะมะ, the best of devotees, because unless one is very much elevated in devotional service, one cannot feel ecstasy from hearing more and more and appreciate the topics as ever fresher and newer.

Text 2

Devanagari

सतामयं सारभृतां निसर्गो
यदर्थवाणीश्रुतिचेतसामपि ।
प्रतिक्षणं नव्यवदच्युतस्य यत्
स्त्रिया विटानामिव साधुवार्ता ॥ २ ॥

Text

satām ayaṁ sāra-bhṛtāṁ nisargo
yad-artha-vāṇī-śruti-cetasām api
prati-kṣaṇaṁ navya-vad acyutasya yat
striyā viṭānām iva sādhu vārtā
สตามฺ อยํ สาร-ภฺฤตำ นิสรฺโค
สะตาม อะยัง สาระ-ภฤตาง นิสัรโค
ยทฺ-อรฺถ-วาณี-ศฺรุติ-เจตสามฺ อปิ
ยัท-อัรถะ-วาณี-ศรุติ-เจตะสาม อะปิ
ปฺรติ-กฺษณํ นวฺย-วทฺ อจฺยุตสฺย ยตฺ
ประติ-กษะณัง นัวยะ-วัท อัจยุตัสยะ ยัต
สฺตฺริยา วิฏานามฺ อิว สาธุ วารฺตา
สตริยา วิฏานาม อิวะ สาธุ วารตา

Synonyms

satām — of the devotees; ayam — this; sāra-bhṛtām — those who are paramahaṁsas, who have accepted the essence of life; nisargaḥ — feature or symptom; yat — which; artha-vāṇī — the aim of life, the aim of profit; śruti — the aim of understanding; cetasām api — who have decided to accept the bliss of transcendental subjects as the aim and object of life; prati-kṣaṇam — every moment; navya-vat — as if newer and newer; acyutasya — of Lord Kṛṣṇa; yat — because; striyāḥ — (topics) of woman or sex; viṭānām — of debauchees, who are attached to women; iva — exactly like; sādhu vārtā — actual conversation.

สตามฺ - สะตาม — of the devotees; อยมฺ - อะยัม — this; สาร - สาระ-ภฺฤตามฺ - ภฤตาม — those who are ปรมหํสสฺ, - ปะระมะหังสัส, who have accepted the essence of life; นิสรฺคห์ - นิสัรคะห์ — feature or symptom; ยตฺ - ยัต — which; อรฺถ - อัรถะ-วาณี - วาณี — the aim of life, the aim of profit; ศฺรุติ - ศรุติ — the aim of understanding; เจตสามฺ - เจตะสาม อปิ - อะปิ — who have decided to accept the bliss of transcendental subjects as the aim and object of life; ปฺรติ - ประติ-กฺษณมฺ - กษะณัม — every moment; นวฺย - นัวยะ-วตฺ - วัต — as if newer and newer; อจฺยุตสฺย - อัจยุตัสยะ — of Lord Kṛṣṇa; ยตฺ - ยัต — because; สฺตฺริยาห์ - สตริยาห์ — (topics) of woman or sex; วิฏานามฺ - วิฏานาม — of debauchees, who are attached to women; อิว - อิวะ — exactly like; สาธุ - สาธุ วารฺตา - วารตา — actual conversation.

Translation

Paramahaṁsas, devotees who have accepted the essence of life, are attached to Kṛṣṇa in the core of their hearts, and He is the aim of their lives. It is their nature to talk only of Kṛṣṇa at every moment, as if such topics were newer and newer. They are attached to such topics, just as materialists are attached to topics of women and sex.

Purport

The word sāra-bhṛtām - สาร-ภฺฤตามฺ - สาระ-ภฤตาม means paramahaṁsas. - ปรมหํสสฺฯ - ปะระมะหังสัสฯ The haṁsa, - หํส, - หังสะ, or swan, accepts milk from a mixture of milk and water and rejects the water. Similarly, the nature of persons who have taken to spiritual life and Kṛṣṇa consciousness, understanding Kṛṣṇa to be the life and soul of everyone, is that they cannot give up kṛṣṇa-kathā, - กฺฤษฺณ-กถา, - กฤษณะ-กะถา, or topics about Kṛṣṇa, at any moment. Such paramahaṁsas - ปรมหํสสฺ - ปะระมะหังสัส always see Kṛṣṇa within the core of the heart (santaḥ sadaiva hṛdayeṣu vilokayanti - สนฺตห์ สไทว หฺฤทเยษุ วิโลกยนฺติ - สันตะห์ สะไทวะ หฤทะเยษุ วิโลกะยันติ). Kāma - กาม - กามะ (desires), krodha - โกฺรธ - กโรธะ (anger) and bhaya - ภย - ภะยะ (fear) are always present in the material world, but in the spiritual, or transcendental, world one can use them for Kṛṣṇa. Kāmaṁ kṛṣṇa-karmārpaṇe - กามํ กฺฤษฺณ-กรฺมารฺปเณ - กามัง กฤษณะ-กัรมารปะเณ. The desire of the paramahaṁsas, - ปรมหํสสฺ, - ปะระมะหังสัส, therefore, is to act always for Kṛṣṇa. Krodhaṁ bhakta-dveṣi jane. - โกฺรธํ ภกฺต-เทฺวษิ ชเนฯ - กโรธัง ภักตะ-ทเวษิ ชะเนฯ They use anger against the nondevotees and transform bhaya, - ภย, - ภะยะ, or fear, into fear of being deviated from Kṛṣṇa consciousness. In this way, the life of a paramahaṁsa - ปรมหํส - ปะระมะหังสะ devotee is used entirely for Kṛṣṇa, just as the life of a person attached to the material world is used simply for women and money. What is day for the materialistic person is night for the spiritualist. What is very sweet for the materialist — namely women and money — is regarded as poison by the spiritualist.

sandarśanaṁ viṣayinām atha yoṣitāṁ ca
ha hanta hanta viṣa-bhakṣaṇato ’py asādhu
สนฺทรฺศนํ วิษยินามฺ อถ โยษิตำ จ
สันทัรศะนัง วิษะยินาม อะถะ โยษิตาง จะ
ห หนฺต หนฺต วิษ-ภกฺษณโต ’ปฺยฺ อสาธุ
หะ หันตะ หันตะ วิษะ-ภักษะณะโต ’ปย อะสาธุ

This is the instruction of Caitanya Mahāprabhu. For the paramahaṁsa, - ปรมหํส, - ปะระมะหังสะ, Kṛṣṇa is everything, but for the materialist, women and money are everything.

Synonyms

śṛṇusva — please hear; avahitaḥ — with great attention; rājan — O King (Mahārāja Parīkṣit); api — although; guhyam — very confidential (because ordinary men cannot understand the activities of Kṛṣṇa); vadāmi — I shall explain; te — unto you; brūyuḥ — explain; snigdhasya — submissive; śiṣyasya — of a disciple; guravaḥ — spiritual masters; guhyam — very confidential; api uta — even so.

ศฺฤณุสฺว - ศฤณุสวะ — please hear; อวหิตห์ - อะวะหิตะห์ — with great atเต - เตntion; ราชนฺ - ราชัน — O King (Mahārāja Parīkṣit); อปิ - อะปิ — although; คุหฺยมฺ - คุหยัม — very confidential (because ordinary men cannot understand the activities of Kṛṣṇa); วทามิ - วะทามิ — I shall explain; te — unto you; พฺรูยุห์ - พรูยุห์ — explain; สฺนิคฺธสฺย - สนิคธัสยะ — submissive; ศิษฺยสฺย - ศิษยัสยะ — of a disciple; คุรวห์ - คุระวะห์ — spiritual masters; คุหฺยมฺ - คุหยัม — very confidential; อปิ - อะปิ อุต - อุตะ — even so.

Translation

O King, kindly hear me with great attention. Although the activities of the Supreme Lord are very confidential, no ordinary man being able to understand them, I shall speak about them to you, for spiritual masters explain to a submissive disciple even subject matters that are very confidential and difficult to understand.

ตถา - ตะถา — thereafter; อฆ - อะฆะ-วทนาตฺ - วะทะนาต — from the mouth of Aghāsura; มฺฤโตฺยห์ - มฤตโยห์ — death personified; รกฺษิตฺวา - รักษิตวา — after saving; วตฺส - วัตสะ-ปาลกานฺ - ปาละกาน — all the cowherd boys and calves; สริตฺ - สะริต-ปุลินมฺ - ปุลินัม — to the bank of the river; อานีย - อานียะ — bringing them; ภควานฺ - ภะคะวาน — the Supreme Personality of Godhead, Kṛṣṇa; อิทมฺ - อิทัม — these words; อพฺรวีตฺ - อัพระวีต — spoke.

Translation

Then, after saving the boys and calves from the mouth of Aghāsura, who was death personified, Lord Kṛṣṇa, the Supreme Personality of Godhead, brought them all to the bank of the river and spoke the following words.

aho — oh; ati-ramyam — very, very beautiful; pulinam — the bank of the river; vayasyāḥ — My dear friends; sva-keli-sampat — full with all paraphernalia for pastimes of play; mṛdula-accha-bālukam — the very soft and clean sandy bank; sphuṭat — in full bloom; saraḥ-gandha — by the aroma of the lotus flower; hṛta — attracted; ali — of the bumblebees; patrika — and of the birds; dhvani-pratidhvāna — the sounds of their chirping and moving and the echoes of these sounds; lasat — moving all over; druma-ākulam — full of nice trees.

อลิ - อะลิ" class="r r-lang-en r-synonyms">

อโห - อะโห — oh; อติ - อะติ-รมฺยมฺ - รัมยัม — very, very beautiful; ปุลินมฺ - ปุลินัม — the bank of the river; วยสฺยาห์ - วะยัสยาห์ — My dear friends; สฺว - สวะ-เกลิ - เกลิ-สมฺปตฺ - สัมปัต — full with all paraphernalia for pastimes of play; มฺฤทุล - มฤทุละ-อจฺฉ - อัจฉะ-พาลุกมฺ - พาลุกัม — the very soft and clean sandy bank; สฺผุฏตฺ - สผุฏัต — in full bloom; สรห์ - สะระห์-คนฺธ - คันธะ — by the aroma of the lotus flower; หฺฤต - หฤตะ — attracted; ali — of the bumblebees; ปตฺริก - ปัตริกะ — and of the birds; ธฺวนิ - ธวะนิ-ปฺรติธฺวาน - ประติธวานะ — the sounds of their chirping and moving and the echoes of these sounds; ลสตฺ - ละสัต — moving all over; ทฺรุม - ทรุมะ-อากุลมฺ - อากุลัม — full of nice trees.

Translation

My dear friends, just see how this riverbank is extremely beautiful because of its pleasing atmosphere. And just see how the blooming lotuses are attracting bees and birds by their aroma. The humming and chirping of the bees and birds is echoing throughout the beautiful trees in the forest. Also, here the sands are clean and soft. Therefore, this must be considered the best place for our sporting and pastimes.

Purport

The description of Vṛndāvana forest as given herewith was spoken by Kṛṣṇa five thousand years ago, and the same condition prevailed during the time of the Vaiṣṇava ācāryas - อาจารฺยสฺ - อาจารยัส three or four hundred years ago. Kūjat-kokila-haṁsa-sārasa-gaṇākīrṇe mayūrākule. - กูชตฺ-โกกิล-หํส-สารส-คณากีรฺเณ มยูรากุเลฯ - กูชัต-โกกิละ-หังสะ-สาระสะ-คะณากีรเณ มะยูรากุเลฯ Vṛndāvana forest is always filled with the chirping and cooing of birds like cuckoos (kokila - โกกิล - โกกิละ), ducks (haṁsa - หํส - หังสะ) and cranes (sārasa - สารส - สาระสะ), and it is also full of peacocks (mayūrākule - มยูรากุเล - มะยูรากุเล). The same sounds and atmosphere still prevail in the area where our Kṛṣṇa-Balarāma temple is situated. Everyone who visits this temple is pleased to hear the chirping of the birds as described here (kūjat-kokila-haṁsa-sārasa - กูชตฺ-โกกิล-หํส-สารส - กูชัต-โกกิละ-หังสะ-สาระสะ).

Text 6

Synonyms

atra — here, on this spot; bhoktavyam — our lunch should be eaten; asmābhiḥ — by us; diva-ārūḍham — it is very late now; kṣudhā arditāḥ — we are fatigued with hunger; vatsāḥ — the calves; samīpe — nearby; apaḥ — water; pītvā — after drinking; carantu — let them eat; śanakaiḥ — slowly; tṛṇam — the grasses.

อตฺร - อัตระ — here, on this spot; โภกฺตวฺยมฺ - โภกตัวยัม — our lunch should be eaten; อสฺมาภิห์ - อัสมาภิห์ — by us; ทิว - ทิวะ-อารูฒมฺ - อารูฒัม — it is very late now; กฺษุธา - กษุธา อรฺทิตาห์ - อัรทิตาห์ — we are fatigued with hunger; วตฺสาห์ - วัตสาห์ — the calves; สมีเป - สะมีเป — nearby; อปห์ - อะปะห์ — water; ปีตฺวา - ปีตวา — after drinking; จรนฺตุ - จะรันตุ — let them eat; ศนไกห์ - ศะนะไกห์ — slowly; ตฺฤณมฺ - ตฤณัม — the grasses.

Translation

I think we should take our lunch here, since we are already hungry because the time is very late. Here the calves may drink water and go slowly here and there and eat the grass.

Synonyms

tathā iti — as Kṛṣṇa proposed, the other cowherd boys agreed; pāyayitvā arbhāḥ — they allowed to drink water; vatsān — the calves; ārudhya — tying them to the trees, allowed them to eat; śādvale — in a place of green, tender grasses; muktvā — opening; śikyāni — their bags of eatables and other paraphernalia; bubhujuḥ — went and enjoyed; samam — equally; bhagavatā — with the Supreme Personality of Godhead; mudā — in transcendental pleasure.

ตถา - ตะถา อิติ - อิติ — as Kṛṣṇa proposed, the other cowherd boys agreed; ปายยิตฺวา - ปายะยิตวา อรฺภาห์ - อัรภาห์ — they allowed to drink water; วตฺสานฺ - วัตสาน — the calves; อารุธฺย - อารุธยะ — tying them to the trees, allowed them to eat; ศาทฺวเล - ศาทวะเล — in a place of green, tender grasses; มุกฺตฺวา - มุกตวา — opening; ศิกฺยานิ - ศิกยานิ — their bags of eatables and other paraphernalia; พุภุชุห์ - พุภุชุห์ — went and enjoyed; สมมฺ - สะมัม — equally; ภควตา - ภะคะวะตา — with the Supreme Personality of Godhead; มุทา - มุทา — in transcendental pleasure.

Translation

Accepting Lord Kṛṣṇa’s proposal, the cowherd boys allowed the calves to drink water from the river and then tied them to trees where there was green, tender grass. Then the boys opened their baskets of food and began eating with Kṛṣṇa in great transcendental pleasure.

Text 8

Devanagari

कृष्णस्य विष्वक् पुरुराजिमण्डलै-
रभ्यानना: फुल्लद‍ृशो व्रजार्भका: ।
सहोपविष्टा विपिने विरेजु-

Text

kṛṣṇasya viṣvak puru-rāji-maṇḍalair

chadā yathāmbhoruha-karṇikāyāḥ

อัภยานะนาห์ ผุลละ-ทฤโศ วระชารภะกาห์

Synonyms

kṛṣṇasya viṣvak — surrounding Kṛṣṇa; puru-rāji-maṇḍalaiḥ — by different encirclements of associates; abhyānanāḥ — everyone looking forward to the center, where Kṛṣṇa was sitting; phulla-dṛśaḥ — their faces looking very bright because of transcendental pleasure; vraja-arbhakāḥ — all the cowherd boys of Vrajabhūmi; saha-upaviṣṭāḥ — sitting with Kṛṣṇa; vipine — in the forest; virejuḥ — so nicely and beautifully made; chadāḥ — petals and leaves; yathā — just as; ambhoruha — of a lotus flower; karṇikāyāḥ — of the whorl.

กฺฤษฺณสฺย - กฤษณัสยะ วิษฺวกฺ - วิษวัก — surrounding Kṛṣṇa; ปุรุ - ปุรุ-ราชิ - ราชิ-มณฺฑไลห์ - มัณฑะไลห์ — by different encirclements of associates; อภฺยานนาห์ - อัภยานะนาห์ — everyone looking forward to the center, where Kṛṣṇa was sitting; ผุลฺล - ผุลละ-ทฺฤศห์ - ทฤศะห์ — their faces looking very bright because of transcendental pleasure; วฺรช - วระชะ-อรฺภกาห์ - อัรภะกาห์ — all the cowherd boys of Vrajabhūmi; สห - สะหะ-อุปวิษฺฏาห์ - อุปะวิษฏาห์ — sitting with Kṛṣṇa; วิปิเน - วิปิเน — in the forest; วิเรชุห์ - วิเรชุห์ — so nicely and beautifully made; ฉทาห์ - ฉะทาห์ — petals and leaves; ยถา - ยะถา — just as; อมฺโภรุห - อัมโภรุหะ — of a lotus flower; กรฺณิกายาห์ - กัรณิกายาห์ — of the whorl.

Translation

Like the whorl of a lotus flower surrounded by its petals and leaves, Kṛṣṇa sat in the center, encircled by lines of His friends, who all looked very beautiful. Every one of them was trying to look forward toward Kṛṣṇa, thinking that Kṛṣṇa might look toward him. In this way they all enjoyed their lunch in the forest.

Purport

To a pure devotee, Kṛṣṇa is always visible, as stated in the Brahma- saṁhitā - พฺรหฺม- สํหิตา - พรัหมะ- สังหิตา (santaḥ sadaiva hṛdayeṣu vilokayanti - สนฺตห์ สไทว หฺฤทเยษุ วิโลกยนฺติ - สันตะห์ สะไทวะ หฤทะเยษุ วิโลกะยันติ) and as indicated by Kṛṣṇa Himself in Bhagavad-gītā - ภควทฺ-คีตา - ภะคะวัท-คีตา (sarvataḥ pāṇi-pādaṁ tat sarvato ’kṣi-śiro-mukham - สรฺวตห์ ปาณิ-ปาทํ ตตฺ สรฺวโต ’กฺษิ-ศิโร-มุขมฺ - สัรวะตะห์ ปาณิ-ปาทัง ตัต สัรวะโต ’กษิ-ศิโร-มุขัม). If by accumulating pious activities (kṛta-puṇya-puñjāḥ - กฺฤต-ปุณฺย-ปุญฺชาห์ - กฤตะ-ปุณยะ-ปุญชาห์) one is raised to the platform of pure devotional service, Kṛṣṇa is always visible in the core of one’s heart. One who has attained such perfection is all-beautiful in transcendental bliss. The present Kṛṣṇa consciousness movement is an attempt to keep Kṛṣṇa in the center, for if this is done all activities will automatically become beautiful and blissful.

Translation

Among the cowherd boys, some placed their lunch on flowers, some on leaves, fruits, or bunches of leaves, some actually in their baskets, some on the bark of trees and some on rocks. This is what the children imagined to be their plates as they ate their lunch.

สเรฺว - สัรเว — all the cowherd boys; มิถห์ - มิถะห์ — to one another; ทรฺศยนฺตห์ - ทัรศะยันตะห์ — showing; สฺว - สวะ-สฺว - สวะ-โภชฺย - โภชยะ-รุจิมฺ - รุจิม ปฺฤถกฺ - ปฤถัก — different varieties of foodstuffs brought from home, with their separate and different tastes; หสนฺตห์ - หะสันตะห์ — after tasting, they were all laughing; หาสยนฺตห์ - หาสะยันตะห์ จ - จะ — and making others laugh; อภฺยวชหฺรุห์ - อัภยะวะชัหรุห์ — enjoyed lunch; สห - สะหะ-อีศฺวราห์ - อีศวะราห์ — along with Kṛṣṇa.

Translation

All the cowherd boys enjoyed their lunch with Kṛṣṇa, showing one another the different tastes of the different varieties of preparations they had brought from home. Tasting one another’s preparations, they began to laugh and make one another laugh.

Purport

Sometimes one friend would say, “Kṛṣṇa, see how my food is relishable,” and Kṛṣṇa would take some and laugh. Similarly, Balarāma, Sudāmā and other friends would taste one another’s food and laugh. In this way, the friends very jubilantly began to eat their respective preparations brought from home.

ติษฐัน มัธเย สวะ-ปะริสุหฤโท หาสะยัน นัรมะภิห์ สไวห์
สฺวรฺเค โลเก มิษติ พุภุเช ยชฺญ-ภุคฺ พาล-เกลิห์
สวัรเค โลเก มิษะติ พุภุเช ยัชญะ-ภุค พาละ-เกลิห์

Synonyms

bibhrat veṇum — keeping the flute; jaṭhara-paṭayoḥ — between the tight clothing and the abdomen; śṛṅga-vetre — both the horn bugle and the cow-driving stick; ca — also; kakṣe — on the waist; vāme — on the left-hand side; pāṇau — taking in hand; masṛṇa-kavalam — very nice food prepared with rice and first-class curd; tat-phalāni — suitable pieces of fruit like bael; aṅgulīṣu — between the fingers; tiṣṭhan — staying in this way; madhye — in the middle; sva-pari-suhṛdaḥ — His own personal associates; hāsayan — making them laugh; narmabhiḥ — with joking words; svaiḥ — His own; svarge loke miṣati — while the inhabitants of the heavenly planets, Svargaloka, were watching this wonderful scene; bubhuje — Kṛṣṇa enjoyed; yajña-bhuk bāla-keliḥ — although He accepts offerings in yajña, for the sake of childhood pastimes He was enjoying foodstuffs very jubilantly with His cowherd boyfriends.

พิภฺรตฺ - พิภรัต เวณุมฺ - เวณุม — keeping the flute; ชฐร - ชะฐะระ-ปฏโยห์ - ปะฏะโยห์ — between the tight clothing and the abdomen; ศฺฤงฺค - ศฤงคะ-เวเตฺร - เวตเร — both the horn bugle and the cow-driving stick; จ - จะ — also; กกฺเษ - กักเษ — on the waist; วาเม - วาเม — on the left-hand side; ปาเณา - ปาเณา — taking in hand; มสฺฤณ - มัสฤณะ-กวลมฺ - กะวะลัม — very nice food prepared with rice and first-class curd; ตตฺ - ตัต-ผลานิ - ผะลานิ — suitable pieces of fruit like bael; องฺคุลีษุ - อังคุลีษุ — between the fingers; ติษฺฐนฺ - ติษฐัน — staying in this way; มเธฺย - มัธเย — in the middle; สฺว - สวะ-ปริ - ปะริ-สุหฺฤทห์ - สุหฤทะห์ — His own personal associates; หาสยนฺ - หาสะยัน — making them laugh; นรฺมภิห์ - นัรมะภิห์ — with joking words; ไสฺวห์ - สไวห์ — His own; สฺวรฺเค - สวัรเค โลเก - โลเก มิษติ - มิษะติ — while the inhabitants of the heavenly planets, Svargaloka, were watching this wonderful scene; พุภุเช - พุภุเช — Kṛṣṇa enjoyed; ยชฺญ - ยัชญะ-ภุกฺ - ภุก พาล - พาละ-เกลิห์ - เกลิห์ — although He accepts offerings in ยชฺญ, - ยัชญะ, for the sake of childhood pastimes He was enjoying foodstuffs very jubilantly with His cowherd boyfriends.

Translation

Kṛṣṇa is yajña-bhuk — that is, He eats only offerings of yajña — but to exhibit His childhood pastimes, He now sat with His flute tucked between His waist and His tight cloth on His right side and with His horn bugle and cow-driving stick on His left. Holding in His hand a very nice preparation of yogurt and rice, with pieces of suitable fruit between His fingers, He sat like the whorl of a lotus flower, looking forward toward all His friends, personally joking with them and creating jubilant laughter among them as He ate. At that time, the denizens of heaven were watching, struck with wonder at how the Personality of Godhead, who eats only in yajña, was now eating with His friends in the forest.

Purport

When Kṛṣṇa was eating with His cowherd boyfriends, a certain bumblebee came there to take part in the eating. Thus Kṛṣṇa joked, “Why have you come to disturb My brāhmaṇa - พฺราหฺมณ - พราหมะณะ friend Madhumaṅgala? You want to kill a brāhmaṇa. - พฺราหฺมณฯ - พราหมะณะฯ This is not good.” All the boys would laugh and enjoy, speaking such joking words while eating. Thus the inhabitants of the higher planets were astonished at how the Supreme Personality of Godhead, who eats only when yajña - ยชฺญ - ยัชญะ is offered, was now eating like an ordinary child with His friends in the forest.

Translation

O Mahārāja Parīkṣit, while the cowherd boys, who knew nothing within the core of their hearts but Kṛṣṇa, were thus engaged in eating their lunch in the forest, the calves went far away, deep into the forest, being allured by green grass.

Text 13

Devanagari

मित्राण्याशान्मा विरमतेहानेष्ये वत्सकानहम् ॥ १३ ॥

Synonyms

tān — that those calves were going away; dṛṣṭvā — seeing; bhaya-santrastān — to the cowherd boys, who were disturbed by fear that within the dense forest the calves would be attacked by some ferocious animals; ūce — Kṛṣṇa said; kṛṣṇaḥ asya bhī-bhayam — Kṛṣṇa, who is Himself the fearful element of all kinds of fear (when Kṛṣṇa is present, there is no fear); mitrāṇi — My dear friends; āśāt — from your enjoyment of eating; mā viramata — do not stop; iha — in this place, in this spot; āneṣye — I shall bring back; vatsakān — the calves; aham — I.

ตานฺ - ตาน — that those calves were going away; ทฺฤษฺฏฺวา - ทฤษฏวา — seeing; ภย - ภะยะ-สนฺตฺรสฺตานฺ - สันตรัสตาน — to the cowherd boys, who were disturbed by fear that within the dense forest the calves would be attacked by some ferocious animals; อูเจ - อูเจ — Kṛṣṇa said; กฺฤษฺณห์ - กฤษณะห์ อสฺย - อัสยะ ภี - ภี-ภยมฺ - ภะยัม — Kṛṣṇa, who is Himself the fearful element of all kinds of fear (when Kṛṣṇa is present, there is no fear); มิตฺราณิ - มิตราณิ — My dear friends; อาศาตฺ - อาศาต — from your enjoyment of eating; มา - มา วิรมต - วิระมะตะ — do not stop; อิห - อิหะ — in this place, in this spot; อาเนเษฺย - อาเนษเย — I shall bring back; วตฺสกานฺ - วัตสะกาน — the calves; อหมฺ - อะหัม — I.

Translation

When Kṛṣṇa saw that His friends the cowherd boys were frightened, He, the fierce controller even of fear itself, said, just to mitigate their fear, “My dear friends, do not stop eating. I shall bring your calves back to this spot by personally going after them Myself.”

Purport

In the presence of Kṛṣṇa’s friendship, a devotee cannot have any fear. Kṛṣṇa is the supreme controller, the controller of even death, which is supposed to be the ultimate fear in this material world. Bhayaṁ dvitīyābhiniveśataḥ syāt - ภยํ ทฺวิตียาภินิเวศตห์ สฺยาตฺ - ภะยัง ทวิตียาภินิเวศะตะห์ สยาต (Bhāg. - ภาคฺฯ - ภาคฯ 11.2.37). This fear arises because of lack of Kṛṣṇa consciousness; otherwise there cannot be any fear. For one who has taken shelter of the lotus feet of Kṛṣṇa, this material world of fear becomes hardly dangerous at all.

bhavāmbudhir vatsa-padaṁ paraṁ padaṁ
padaṁ padaṁ yad vipadāṁ na teṣām
ภวามฺพุธิรฺ วตฺส-ปทํ ปรํ ปทํ
ภะวามพุธิร วัตสะ-ปะทัง ปะรัง ปะทัง
ปทํ ปทํ ยทฺ วิปทำ น เตษามฺ
ปะทัง ปะทัง ยัท วิปะทาง นะ เตษาม

Bhavāmbudhiḥ, - ภวามฺพุธิห์, - ภะวามพุธิห์, the material ocean of fear, becomes very easy to cross by the mercy of the supreme controller. This material world, in which there is fear and danger at every step (padaṁ padaṁ yad vipadām - ปทํ ปทํ ยทฺ วิปทามฺ - ปะทัง ปะทัง ยัท วิปะทาม), is not meant for those who have taken shelter at Kṛṣṇa’s lotus feet. Such persons are delivered from this fearful world.

samāśritā ye pada-pallava-plavaṁ
mahat-padaṁ puṇya-yaśo murāreḥ
bhavāmbudhir vatsa-padaṁ paraṁ padaṁ
padaṁ padaṁ yad vipadāṁ na teṣām
สมาศฺริตา เย ปท-ปลฺลว-ปฺลวํ
สะมาศริตา เย ปะทะ-ปัลละวะ-ปละวัง
มหตฺ-ปทํ ปุณฺย-ยโศ มุราเรห์
มะหัต-ปะทัง ปุณยะ-ยะโศ มุราเรห์
ภวามฺพุธิรฺ วตฺส-ปทํ ปรํ ปทํ
ภะวามพุธิร วัตสะ-ปะทัง ปะรัง ปะทัง
ปทํ ปทํ ยทฺ วิปทำ น เตษามฺ
ปะทัง ปะทัง ยัท วิปะทาง นะ เตษาม

(Bhāg. 10.14.58)

Everyone, therefore, should take shelter of the Supreme Person, who is the source of fearlessness, and thus be secure.

Text 14

Devanagari

इत्युक्त्वाद्रिदरीकुञ्जगह्वरेष्वात्मवत्सकान् ।
विचिन्वन्भगवान्कृष्ण: सपाणिकवलो ययौ ॥ १४ ॥

Text

ity uktvādri-darī-kuñja-
gahvareṣv ātma-vatsakān
vicinvan bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ
sapāṇi-kavalo yayau
อิตฺยฺ อุกฺตฺวาทฺริ-ทรี-กุญฺช-
อิตย อุกตวาทริ-ทะรี-กุญชะ-
คหฺวเรษฺวฺ อาตฺม-วตฺสกานฺ
คัหวะเรษว อาตมะ-วัตสะกาน
วิจินฺวนฺ ภควานฺ กฺฤษฺณห์
วิจินวัน ภะคะวาน กฤษณะห์
สปาณิ-กวโล ยเยา
สะปาณิ-กะวะโล ยะเยา

Synonyms

iti uktvā — saying this (“Let Me bring your calves personally”); adri-darī-kuñja-gahvareṣu — everywhere in the mountains, the mountain caves, the bushes and narrow places; ātma-vatsakān — the calves belonging to His own personal friends; vicinvan — searching out; bhagavān — the Supreme Personality of Godhead; kṛṣṇaḥ — Lord Kṛṣṇa; sa-pāṇi-kavalaḥ — carrying His yogurt and rice in His hand; yayau — started out.

อิติ - อิติ อุกฺตฺวา - อุกตวา — ส - สะying this (“Let Me bring your calves personally”); อทฺริ - อัทริ-ทรี - ทะรี-กุญฺช - กุญชะ-คหฺวเรษุ - คัหวะเรษุ — everywhere in the mountains, the mountain caves, the bushes and narrow places; อาตฺม - อาตมะ-วตฺสกานฺ - วัตสะกาน — the calves belonging to His own personal friends; วิจินฺวนฺ - วิจินวัน — searching out; ภควานฺ - ภะคะวาน — the Supreme Personality of Godhead; กฺฤษฺณห์ - กฤษณะห์ — Lord Kṛṣṇa; sa-ปาณิ - ปาณิ-กวลห์ - กะวะละห์ — carrying His yogurt and rice in His hand; ยเยา - ยะเยา — started out.

Translation

“Let Me go and search for the calves,” Kṛṣṇa said. “Don’t disturb your enjoyment.” Then, carrying His yogurt and rice in His hand, the Supreme Personality of Godhead, Kṛṣṇa, immediately went out to search for the calves of His friends. To please His friends, He began searching in all the mountains, mountain caves, bushes and narrow passages.

Purport

The Vedas - เวทสฺ - เวทัส (Śvetāśvatara Upaniṣad - เศฺวตาศฺวตร อุปนิษทฺ - ศเวตาศวะตะระ อุปะนิษัท 6.8) assert that the Supreme Personality of Godhead has nothing to do personally (na tasya kāryaṁ karaṇaṁ ca vidyate - น ตสฺย การฺยํ กรณํ จ วิทฺยเต - นะ ตัสยะ การยัง กะระณัง จะ วิทยะเต) because He is doing everything through His energies and potencies (parāsya śaktir vividhaiva śrūyate - ปราสฺย ศกฺติรฺ วิวิไธว ศฺรูยเต - ปะราสยะ ศักติร วิวิไธวะ ศรูยะเต). Nonetheless, here we see that He took personal care to find the calves of His friends. This was Kṛṣṇa’s causeless mercy. Mayādhyakṣeṇa prakṛtiḥ sūyate sa-carācaram: - มยาธฺยกฺเษณ ปฺรกฺฤติห์ สูยเต ส-จราจรมฺ: - มะยาธยักเษณะ ปรักฤติห์ สูยะเต สะ-จะราจะรัม: all the affairs of the entire world and the entire cosmic manifestation are working under His direction, through His different energies. Still, when there is a need to take care of His friends, He does this personally. Kṛṣṇa assured His friends, “Don’t be afraid. I am going personally to search for your calves.” This was Kṛṣṇa’s causeless mercy.

Synonyms

ambhojanma-janiḥ — Lord Brahmā, who was born from a lotus flower; tat-antara-gataḥ — now became entangled with the affairs of Kṛṣṇa, who was enjoying luncheon pastimes with His cowherd boys; māyā-arbhakasya — of the boys made by Kṛṣṇa’s māyā; īśituḥ — of the supreme controller; draṣṭum — just to see; mañju — very pleasing; mahitvam anyat api — other glories of the Lord also; tat-vatsān — their calves; itaḥ — than that place where they were; vatsa-pān — and the cowherd boys taking care of the calves; nītvā — bringing them; anyatra — to a different place; kurūdvaha — O Mahārāja Parīkṣit; antara-dadhāt — kept hidden and invisible for some time; khe avasthitaḥ yaḥ — this person Brahmā, who was situated in the higher planetary system in the sky; purā — formerly; dṛṣṭvā — was observing; aghāsura-mokṣaṇam — the wonderful killing and deliverance of Aghāsura from material tribulation; prabhavataḥ — of the all-potent Supreme Person; prāptaḥ param vismayam — had become extremely astonished.

อมฺโภชนฺม - อัมโภชันมะ-ชนิห์ - ชะนิห์ — Lord Brahmā, who was born from a lotus flower; ตตฺ - ตัต-อนฺตร - อันตะระ-คตห์ - คะตะห์ — now became entangled with the affairs of Kṛṣṇa, who was enjoying luncheon pastimes with His cowherd boys; มายา - มายา-อรฺภกสฺย - อัรภะกัสยะ — of the boys made by Kṛṣṇa’s มายา - มายา; อีศิตุห์ - อีศิตุห์ — of the supreme controller; ทฺรษฺฏุมฺ - ทรัษฏุม — just to see; มญฺชุ - มัญชุ — very pleasing; มหิตฺวมฺ - มะหิตวัม อนฺยตฺ - อันยัต อปิ - อะปิ — other glories of the Lord also; ตตฺ - ตัต-วตฺสานฺ - วัตสาน — their calves; อิตห์ - อิตะห์ — than that place where they were; วตฺส - วัตสะ-ปานฺ - ปาน — and the cowherd boys taking care of the calves; นีตฺวา - นีตวา — bringing them; อนฺยตฺร - อันยัตระ — to a different place; กุรูทฺวห - กุรูทวะหะ — O Mahārāja Parīkṣit; อนฺตร - อันตะระ-ทธาตฺ - ทะธาต — kept hidden and invisible for some time; เข - เข อวสฺถิตห์ - อะวัสถิตะห์ ยห์ - ยะห์ — this person Brahmā, who was situated in the higher planetary system in the sky; ปุรา - ปุรา — formerly; ทฺฤษฺฏฺวา - ทฤษฏวา — was observing; อฆาสุร - อะฆาสุระ-โมกฺษณมฺ - โมกษะณัม — the wonderful killing and deliverance of Aghāsura from material tribulation; ปฺรภวตห์ - ประภะวะตะห์ — of the all-potent Supreme Person; ปฺราปฺตห์ - ปราปตะห์ ปรมฺ - ปะรัม วิสฺมยมฺ - วิสมะยัม — had become extremely astonished.

Translation

O Mahārāja Parīkṣit, Brahmā, who resides in the higher planetary system in the sky, had observed the activities of the most powerful Kṛṣṇa in killing and delivering Aghāsura, and he was astonished. Now that same Brahmā wanted to show some of his own power and see the power of Kṛṣṇa, who was engaged in His childhood pastimes, playing as if with ordinary cowherd boys. Therefore, in Kṛṣṇa’s absence, Brahmā took all the boys and calves to another place. Thus he became entangled, for in the very near future he would see how powerful Kṛṣṇa was.

Purport

When Aghāsura was being killed by Kṛṣṇa, who was accompanied by His associates, Brahmā was astonished, but when he saw that Kṛṣṇa was very much enjoying His pastimes of lunch, he was even more astonished and wanted to test whether Kṛṣṇa was actually there. Thus he became entangled in Kṛṣṇa’s māyā. - มายาฯ - มายาฯ After all, Brahmā was born materially. As mentioned here, ambhojanma janiḥ: - อมฺโภชนฺม ชนิห์: - อัมโภชันมะ ชะนิห์: he was born of ambhoja, - อมฺโภช, - อัมโภชะ, a lotus flower. It does not matter that he was born of a lotus and not of any man, animal or material father. A lotus is also material, and anyone born through the material energy must be subject to the four material deficiencies: bhrama - ภฺรม - ภระมะ (the tendency to commit mistakes), pramāda - ปฺรมาท - ประมาทะ (the tendency to be illusioned), vipralipsā - วิปฺรลิปฺสา - วิประลิปสา (the tendency to cheat) and karaṇāpāṭava - กรณาปาฏว - กะระณาปาฏะวะ (imperfect senses). Thus Brahmā also became entangled.

Brahmā, with his māyā, - มายา, - มายา, wanted to test whether Kṛṣṇa was actually present. These cowherd boys were but expansions of Kṛṣṇa’s personal self (ānanda-cinmaya-rasa-pratibhāvitābhiḥ - อานนฺท-จินฺมย-รส-ปฺรติภาวิตาภิห์ - อานันทะ-จินมะยะ-ระสะ-ประติภาวิตาภิห์). Later Kṛṣṇa would show Brahmā how He expands Himself into everything as His personal pleasure, ānanda-cinmaya-rasa. - อานนฺท-จินฺมย-รสฯ - อานันทะ-จินมะยะ-ระสะฯ Hlādinī śaktir asmāt: - หฺลาทินี ศกฺติรฺ อสฺมาตฺ: - หลาทินี ศักติร อัสมาต: Kṛṣṇa has a transcendental potency called hlādinī śakti. - หฺลาทินี ศกฺติฯ - หลาทินี ศักติฯ He does not enjoy anything that is a product of the material energy. Brahmā, therefore, would see Lord Kṛṣṇa expand His energy.

Brahmā wanted to take away Kṛṣṇa’s associates, but instead he took away some other boys and calves. Rāvaṇa wanted to take away Sītā, but that was impossible, and instead he took away a māyā - มายา - มายา Sītā. Similarly, Brahmā took away māyārbhakāḥ: - มายารฺภกาห์: - มายารภะกาห์: boys manifested by Kṛṣṇa’s māyā. - มายาฯ - มายาฯ Brahmā could show some extraordinary opulence to the māyārbhakāḥ; - มายารฺภกาห์; - มายารภะกาห์; but he could not show any extraordinary potency to Kṛṣṇa’s associates. That he would see in the very near future. Māyārbhakasya īśituḥ. - มายารฺภกสฺย อีศิตุห์ฯ - มายารภะกัสยะ อีศิตุห์ฯ This bewilderment, this māyā, - มายา, - มายา, was caused by the supreme controller, prabhavataḥ - ปฺรภวตห์ - ประภะวะตะห์ — the all-potent Supreme Person, Kṛṣṇa — and we shall see the result. Anyone materially born is subject to bewilderment. This pastime is therefore called brahma-vimohana-līlā, - พฺรหฺม-วิโมหน-ลีลา, - พรัหมะ-วิโมหะนะ-ลีลา, the pastime of bewildering Brahmā. Mohitaṁ nābhijānāti mām ebhyaḥ param avyayam - โมหิตํ นาภิชานาติ มามฺ เอภฺยห์ ปรมฺ อวฺยยมฺ - โมหิตัง นาภิชานาติ มาม เอภยะห์ ปะรัม อัวยะยัม (Bg. 7.13). Materially born persons cannot fully understand Kṛṣṇa. Even the demigods cannot understand Him (muhyanti yat sūrayaḥ - มุหฺยนฺติ ยตฺ สูรยห์ - มุหยันติ ยัต สูระยะห์). Tene brahmā hṛdā ya ādi-kavaye - เตเน พฺรหฺมา หฺฤทา ย อาทิ-กวเย - เตเน พรัหมา หฤทา ยะ อาทิ-กะวะเย (Bhāg. - ภาคฺฯ - ภาคฯ 1.1.1). Everyone, from Brahmā down to the small insect, must take lessons from Kṛṣṇa.

ตตห์ - ตะตะห์ — thereafter; วตฺสานฺ - วัตสาน — the จ - จะlves; อทฺฤษฺฏฺวา - อัทฤษฏวา — not seeing there within the forest; เอตฺย - เอตยะ — after; ปุลิเน - ปุลิเน อปิ - อะปิ — to the bank of the Yamunā; ca — also; วตฺสปานฺ - วัตสะปาน — could not see the cowherd boys; อุเภา - อุเภา อปิ - อะปิ — both of them (the calves and the cowherd boys); วเน - วะเน — within the forest; กฺฤษฺณห์ - กฤษณะห์ — Lord Kṛṣṇa; วิจิกาย - วิจิกายะ — searched all over; สมนฺตตห์ - สะมันตะตะห์ — here and there.

Translation

Thereafter, when Kṛṣṇa was unable to find the calves, He returned to the bank of the river, but there He was also unable to see the cowherd boys. Thus He began to search for both the calves and the boys, as if He could not understand what had happened.

Purport

Kṛṣṇa could immediately understand that Brahmā had taken away both the calves and the boys, but as an innocent child He searched here and there so that Brahmā could not understand Kṛṣṇa’s māyā. - มายาฯ - มายาฯ This was all a dramatic performance. A player knows everything, but still he plays on the stage in such a way that others do not understand him.

Translation

When Kṛṣṇa was unable to find the calves and their caretakers, the cowherd boys, anywhere in the forest, He could suddenly understand that this was the work of Lord Brahmā.

Purport

Although Kṛṣṇa is viśva-vit, - วิศฺว-วิตฺ, - วิศวะ-วิต, the knower of everything happening in the entire cosmic manifestation, as an innocent child He showed ignorance of Brahmā’s actions, although He could immediately understand that these were the doings of Brahmā. This pastime is called brahma-vimohana, - พฺรหฺม-วิโมหน, - พรัหมะ-วิโมหะนะ, the bewilderment of Brahmā. Brahmā was already bewildered by Kṛṣṇa’s activities as an innocent child, and now he would be further bewildered.

Synonyms

tataḥ — thereafter; kṛṣṇaḥ — the Supreme Personality of Godhead; mudam — pleasure; kartum — to create; tat-mātṝṇām ca — of the mothers of the cowherd boys and calves; kasya ca — and (the pleasure) of Brahmā; ubhayāyitam — expansion, both as the calves and as the cowherd boys; ātmānam — Himself; cakre — did; viśva-kṛt īśvaraḥ — it was not difficult for Him, for He is the creator of the whole cosmic manifestation.

ตตห์ - ตะตะห์ — thereafter; กฺฤษฺณห์ - กฤษณะห์ — the Supreme Personality of Godhead; มุทมฺ - มุทัม — pleasure; กรฺตุมฺ - กัรตุม — to create; ตตฺ - ตัต-มาตฺฤๅณามฺ - มาตฤๅณาม จ - จะ — of the mothers of the cowherd boys and จ - จะlves; กสฺย - กัสยะ ca — and (the pleasure) of Brahmā; อุภยายิตมฺ - อุภะยายิตัม — expansion, both as the calves and as the cowherd boys; อาตฺมานมฺ - อาตมานัม — Himself; จเกฺร - จักเร — did; วิศฺว - วิศวะ-กฺฤตฺ - กฤต อีศฺวรห์ - อีศวะระห์ — it was not difficult for Him, for He is the creator of the whole cosmic manifestation.

Translation

Thereafter, just to create pleasure both for Brahmā and for the mothers of the calves and cowherd boys, Kṛṣṇa, the creator of the entire cosmic manifestation, expanded Himself as calves and boys.

Purport

Although Brahmā was already entangled in bewilderment, he wanted to show his power to the cowherd boys; but after he took away the boys and their calves and returned to his abode, Kṛṣṇa created further astonishment for Brahmā, and for the mothers of the boys, by establishing the lunch pastimes in the forest again and replacing all the calves and boys, just as they had appeared before. According to the Vedas, ekaṁ bahu syām: - เวทสฺ, เอกํ พหุ สฺยามฺ: - เวทัส, เอกัง พะหุ สยาม: the Personality of Godhead can become many, many millions upon millions of calves and cowherd boys, as He did to bewilder Brahmā more and more.

Synonyms

yāvat vatsapa — exactly like the cowherd boys; vatsaka-alpaka-vapuḥ — and exactly like the tender bodies of the calves; yāvat kara-aṅghri-ādikam — exactly to the measurement of their particular varieties of legs and hands; yāvat yaṣṭi-viṣāṇa-veṇu-dala-śik — not only like their bodies but exactly like their bugles, flutes, sticks, lunch bags and so on; yāvat vibhūṣā-ambaram — exactly like their ornaments and dress in all their varied particulars; yāvat śīla-guṇa-abhidhā-ākṛti-vayaḥ — their exact character, habits, features, attributes and explicit bodily features; yāvat vihāra-ādikam — exactly according to their tastes or amusements; sarvam — everything in detail; viṣṇu-mayam — expansions of Vāsudeva, Viṣṇu; giraḥ aṅga-vat — voices exactly like theirs; ajaḥ — Kṛṣṇa; sarva-svarūpaḥ babhau — created everything in detail as Himself, without any change.

ยาวตฺ - ยาวัต วตฺสป - วัตสะปะ — exactly like the cowherd boys; วตฺสก - วัตสะกะ-อลฺปก - อัลปะกะ-วปุห์ - วะปุห์ — and exactly like the tender bodies of the calves; ยาวตฺ - ยาวัต กร - กะระ-องฺฆฺริ - อังฆริ-อาทิกมฺ - อาทิกัม — exactly to the measurement of their particular varieties of legs and hands; ยาวตฺ - ยาวัต ยษฺฏิ - ยัษฏิ-วิษาณ - วิษาณะ-เวณุ - เวณุ-ทล - ทะละ-ศิกฺ - ศิก — not only like their bodies but exactly like their bugles, flutes, sticks, lunch bags and so on; ยาวตฺ - ยาวัต วิภูษา - วิภูษา-อมฺพรมฺ - อัมพะรัม — exactly like their ornaments and dress in all their varied particulars; ยาวตฺ - ยาวัต ศีล - ศีละ-คุณ - คุณะ-อภิธา - อะภิธา-อากฺฤติ - อากฤติ-วยห์ - วะยะห์ — their exact character, habits, features, attributes and explicit bodily features; ยาวตฺ - ยาวัต วิหาร - วิหาระ-อาทิกมฺ - อาทิกัม — exactly according to their tastes or amusements; สรฺวมฺ - สัรวัม — everything in detail; วิษฺณุ - วิษณุ-มยมฺ - มะยัม — expansions of Vāsudeva, Viṣṇu; คิรห์ - คิระห์ องฺค - อังคะ-วตฺ - วัต — voices exactly like theirs; อชห์ - อะชะห์ — Kṛṣṇa; สรฺว - สัรวะ-สฺวรูปห์ - สวะรูปะห์ พเภา - พะเภา — created everything in detail as Himself, without any change.

Translation

By His Vāsudeva feature, Kṛṣṇa simultaneously expanded Himself into the exact number of missing cowherd boys and calves, with their exact bodily features, their particular types of hands, legs and other limbs, their sticks, bugles and flutes, their lunch bags, their particular types of dress and ornaments placed in various ways, their names, ages and forms, and their special activities and characteristics. By expanding Himself in this way, beautiful Kṛṣṇa proved the statement samagra-jagad viṣṇumayam: “Lord Viṣṇu is all-pervading.”

Purport

As stated in the Brahma-saṁhitā - พฺรหฺม-สํหิตา - พรัหมะ-สังหิตา (5.33):

advaitam acyutam anādim ananta-rūpam
ādyaṁ purāṇa-puruṣaṁ nava-yauvanaṁ ca
อไทฺวตมฺ อจฺยุตมฺ อนาทิมฺ อนนฺต-รูปมฺ
อัทไวตัม อัจยุตัม อะนาทิม อะนันตะ-รูปัม
อาทฺยํ ปุราณ-ปุรุษํ นว-เยาวนํ จ
อาทยัง ปุราณะ-ปุรุษัง นะวะ-เยาวะนัง จะ

Kṛṣṇa, paraṁ brahma, - ปรํ พฺรหฺม, - ปะรัง พรัหมะ, the Supreme Personality of Godhead, is ādyam, - อาทฺยมฺ, - อาทยัม, the beginning of everything; He is ādi-puruṣam, - อาทิ-ปุรุษมฺ, - อาทิ-ปุรุษัม, the ever-youthful original person. He can expand Himself in more forms than one can imagine, yet He does not fall down from His original form as Kṛṣṇa; therefore He is called Acyuta. This is the Supreme Personality of Godhead. Sarvaṁ viṣṇumayaṁ jagat. - สรฺวํ วิษฺณุมยํ ชคตฺฯ - สัรวัง วิษณุมะยัง ชะคัตฯ Sarvaṁ khalv idaṁ brahma - สรฺวํ ขลฺวฺ อิทํ พฺรหฺม - สัรวัง ขัลว อิทัง พรัหมะ. Kṛṣṇa thus proved that He is everything, that He can become everything, but that still He is personally different from everything (mat-sthāni sarva-bhūtāni na cāhaṁ teṣv avasthitaḥ - มตฺ-สฺถานิ สรฺว-ภูตานิ น จาหํ เตษฺวฺ อวสฺถิตห์ - มัต-สถานิ สัรวะ-ภูตานิ นะ จาหัง เตษว อะวัสถิตะห์). This is Kṛṣṇa, who is understood by acintya-bhedābheda-tattva - อจินฺตฺย-เภทาเภท-ตตฺตฺว - อะจินตยะ-เภทาเภทะ-ตัตตวะ philosophy. Pūrṇasya pūrṇam ādāya pūrṇam evāvaśiṣyate: - ปูรฺณสฺย ปูรฺณมฺ อาทาย ปูรฺณมฺ เอวาวศิษฺยเต: - ปูรณัสยะ ปูรณัม อาทายะ ปูรณัม เอวาวะศิษยะเต: Kṛṣṇa is always complete, and although He can create millions of universes, all of them full in all opulences, He remains as opulent as ever, without any change (advaitam - อไทฺวตมฺ - อัทไวตัม). This is explained by different Vaiṣṇava ācāryas - อาจารฺยสฺ - อาจารยัส through philosophies such as viśuddhādvaita, viśiṣṭādvaita - วิศุทฺธาไทฺวต, วิศิษฺฏาไทฺวต - วิศุทธาทไวตะ, วิศิษฏาทไวตะ and dvaitādvaita. - ไทฺวตาไทฺวตฯ - ทไวตาทไวตะฯ Therefore one must learn about Kṛṣṇa from the ācāryas. - อาจารฺยสฺฯ - อาจารยัสฯ Ācāryavān puruṣo veda: - อาจารฺยวานฺ ปุรุโษ เวท: - อาจารยะวาน ปุรุโษ เวทะ: one who follows the path of the ācāryas - อาจารฺยสฺ - อาจารยัส knows things as they are. Such a person can know Kṛṣṇa as He is, at least to some extent, and as soon as one understands Kṛṣṇa (janma karma ca me divyam evaṁ yo vetti tattvataḥ - ชนฺม กรฺม จ เม ทิวฺยมฺ เอวํ โย เวตฺติ ตตฺตฺวตห์ - ชันมะ กัรมะ จะ เม ทิวยัม เอวัง โย เวตติ ตัตตวะตะห์), one is liberated from material bondage (tyaktvā dehaṁ punar janma naiti mām eti so ’rjuna - ตฺยกฺตฺวา เทหํ ปุนรฺ ชนฺม ไนติ มามฺ เอติ โส ’รฺชุน - ตยักตวา เทหัง ปุนัร ชันมะ ไนติ มาม เอติ โส ’รชุนะ).

Text 20

Devanagari

स्वयमात्मात्मगोवत्सान् प्रतिवार्यात्मवत्सपै: ।
क्रीडन्नात्मविहारैश्च सर्वात्मा प्राविशद् व्रजम् ॥ २० ॥

Text

svayam ātmātma-govatsān
prativāryātma-vatsapaiḥ
krīḍann ātma-vihāraiś ca
sarvātmā prāviśad vrajam
สฺวยมฺ อาตฺมาตฺม-โควตฺสานฺ
สวะยัม อาตมาตมะ-โควัตสาน
ปฺรติวารฺยาตฺม-วตฺสไปห์
ประติวารยาตมะ-วัตสะไปห์
กฺรีฑนฺนฺ อาตฺม-วิหาไรศฺ จ
กรีฑันน อาตมะ-วิหาไรศ จะ
สรฺวาตฺมา ปฺราวิศทฺ วฺรชมฺ
สัรวาตมา ปราวิศัท วระชัม

Synonyms

svayam ātmā — Kṛṣṇa, who is personally the Supreme Soul, the Supersoul; ātma-go-vatsān — now expanded into calves that were also He Himself; prativārya ātma-vatsapaiḥ — again He Himself was represented as the cowherd boys controlling and commanding the calves; krīḍan — thus Himself constituting everything in these transcendental pastimes; ātma-vihāraiḥ ca — enjoying Himself by Himself in different ways; sarva-ātmā — the Supersoul, Kṛṣṇa; prāviśat — entered; vrajam — Vrajabhūmi, the land of Mahārāja Nanda and Yaśodā.

สฺวยมฺ - สวะยัม อาตฺมา - อาตมา — Kṛṣṇa, who is personally the Supreme Soul, the Supersoul; อาตฺม - อาตมะ-โค - โค-วตฺสานฺ - วัตสาน — now expanded into จ - จะlves that were also He Himself; ปฺรติวารฺย - ประติวารยะ อาตฺม - อาตมะ-วตฺสไปห์ - วัตสะไปห์ — again He Himself was represented as the cowherd boys controlling and commanding the calves; กฺรีฑนฺ - กรีฑัน — thus Himself constituting everything in these transcendental pastimes; อาตฺม - อาตมะ-วิหาไรห์ - วิหาไรห์ ca — enjoying Himself by Himself in different ways; สรฺว - สัรวะ-อาตฺมา - อาตมา — the Supersoul, Kṛṣṇa; ปฺราวิศตฺ - ปราวิศัต — entered; วฺรชมฺ - วระชัม — Vrajabhūmi, the land of Mahārāja Nanda and Yaśodā.

Translation

Now expanding Himself so as to appear as all the calves and cowherd boys, all of them as they were, and at the same time appear as their leader, Kṛṣṇa entered Vrajabhūmi, the land of His father, Nanda Mahārāja, just as He usually did while enjoying their company.

Purport

Kṛṣṇa usually stayed in the forest and pasturing ground, taking care of the calves and cows with His associates the cowherd boys. Now that the original group had been taken away by Brahmā, Kṛṣṇa Himself assumed the forms of every member of the group, without anyone’s knowledge, even the knowledge of Baladeva, and continued the usual program. He was ordering His friends to do this and that, and He was controlling the calves and going into the forest to search for them when they went astray, allured by new grass, but these calves and boys were He Himself. This was Kṛṣṇa’s inconceivable potency. As explained by Śrīla Svarūpa Dāmodara Gosvāmī, rādhā kṛṣṇa-praṇaya-vikṛtir hlādinī śaktir asmāt. - ราธา กฺฤษฺณ-ปฺรณย-วิกฺฤติรฺ หฺลาทินี ศกฺติรฺ อสฺมาตฺฯ - ราธา กฤษณะ-ประณะยะ-วิกฤติร หลาทินี ศักติร อัสมาตฯ Rādhā and Kṛṣṇa are the same. Kṛṣṇa, by expanding His pleasure potency, becomes Rādhārāṇī. The same pleasure potency (ānanda-cinmaya-rasa - อานนฺท-จินฺมย-รส - อานันทะ-จินมะยะ-ระสะ) was expanded by Kṛṣṇa when He Himself became all the calves and boys and enjoyed transcendental bliss in Vrajabhūmi. This was done by the Yoga-māyā potency and was inconceivable to persons under the potency of Mahā-māyā.

ตตฺ - ตัต-ตตฺ - ตัต-วตฺสานฺ - วัตสาน — the calves, which belonged to different cows; ปฺฤถกฺ - ปฤถัก — separately; นีตฺวา - นีตวา — bringing; ตตฺ - ตัต-ตตฺ - ตัต-โคษฺเฐ - โคษเฐ — to their respective cow sheds; นิเวศฺย - นิเวศยะ — entering; สห์ - สะห์ — Kṛṣṇa; ตตฺ - ตัต-ตตฺ - ตัต-อาตฺมา - อาตมา — as originally different individual souls; อภวตฺ - อะภะวัต — He expanded Himself in that way; ราชนฺ - ราชัน — O King Parīkṣit; ตตฺ - ตัต-ตตฺ - ตัต-สทฺม - สัทมะ — their respective houses; ปฺรวิษฺฏวานฺ - ประวิษฏะวาน — entered (Kṛṣṇa thus entered everywhere).

Translation

O Mahārāja Parīkṣit, Kṛṣṇa, who had divided Himself as different calves and also as different cowherd boys, entered different cow sheds as the calves and then different homes as different boys.

Purport

Kṛṣṇa had many, many friends, of whom Śrīdāmā, Sudāmā and Subala were prominent. Thus Kṛṣṇa Himself became Śrīdāmā, Sudāmā and Subala and entered their respective houses with their respective calves.

tat-mātaraḥ — the mothers of the respective cowherd boys; veṇu-rava — because of the sounds played on flutes and bugles by the cowherd boys; tvara — immediately; utthitāḥ — awakened from their respective household duties; utthāpya — immediately lifted their respective sons; dorbhiḥ — with their two arms; parirabhya — embracing; nirbharam — without feeling any weight; sneha-snuta — which was flowing because of intense love; stanya-payaḥ — their breast milk; sudhā-āsavam — tasting just like a nectarean beverage; matvā — accepting the milk like that; param — the Supreme; brahma — Kṛṣṇa; sutān apāyayan — began to feed their respective sons.

ตตฺ - ตัต-มาตรห์ - มาตะระห์ — the mothers of the respective cowherd boys; เวณุ - เวณุ-รว - ระวะ — because of the sounds played on flutes and bugles by the cowherd boys; ตฺวร - ตวะระ — immediately; อุตฺถิตาห์ - อุตถิตาห์ — awakened from their respective household duties; อุตฺถาปฺย - อุตถาปยะ — immediately lifted their respective sons; โทรฺภิห์ - โทรภิห์ — with their two arms; ปริรภฺย - ปะริรัภยะ — embracing; นิรฺภรมฺ - นิรภะรัม — without feeling any weight; เสฺนห - สเนหะ-สฺนุต - สนุตะ — which was flowing because of intense love; สฺตนฺย - สตันยะ-ปยห์ - ปะยะห์ — their breast milk; สุธา - สุธา-อาสวมฺ - อาสะวัม — tasting just like a nectarean beverage; มตฺวา - มัตวา — accepting the milk like that; ปรมฺ - ปะรัม — the Supreme; พฺรหฺม - พรัหมะ — Kṛṣṇa; สุตานฺ - สุตาน อปายยนฺ - อะปายะยัน — began to feed their respective sons.

Translation

The mothers of the boys, upon hearing the sounds of the flutes and bugles being played by their sons, immediately rose from their household tasks, lifted their boys onto their laps, embraced them with both arms and began to feed them with their breast milk, which flowed forth because of extreme love specifically for Kṛṣṇa. Actually Kṛṣṇa is everything, but at that time, expressing extreme love and affection, they took special pleasure in feeding Kṛṣṇa, the Parabrahman, and Kṛṣṇa drank the milk from His respective mothers as if it were a nectarean beverage.

Purport

Although all the elderly gopīs - โคปีสฺ - โคปีส knew that Kṛṣṇa was the son of mother Yaśodā, they still desired, “If Kṛṣṇa had become my son, I would also have taken care of Him like mother Yaśodā.” This was their inner ambition. Now, in order to please them, Kṛṣṇa personally took the role of their sons and fulfilled their desire. They enhanced their special love for Kṛṣṇa by embracing Him and feeding Him, and Kṛṣṇa tasted their breast milk to be just like a nectarean beverage. While thus bewildering Brahmā, He enjoyed the special transcendental pleasure created by yoga-māyā - โยค-มายา - โยคะ-มายา between all the other mothers and Himself.

tataḥ — thereafter; nṛpa — O King (Mahārāja Parīkṣit); unmardana — by massaging them with oil; majja — by bathing; lepana — by smearing the body with oil and sandalwood pulp; alaṅkāra — by decorating with ornaments; rakṣā — by chanting protective mantras; tilaka — by decorating the body with tilaka marks in twelve places; aśana-ādibhiḥ — and by feeding them sumptuously; saṁlālitaḥ — in this way cared for by the mothers; sva-ācaritaiḥ — by their characteristic behavior; praharṣa-yan — making the mothers very much pleased; sāyam — evening; gataḥ — arrived; yāma-yamena — as the time of each activity passed; mādhavaḥ — Lord Kṛṣṇa.

ตตห์ - ตะตะห์ — thereafter; นฺฤป - นฤปะ — O King (Mahārāja Parīkṣit); อุนฺมรฺทน - อุนมัรทะนะ — by massaging them with oil; มชฺช - มัชชะ — by bathing; เลปน - เลปะนะ — by smearing the body with oil and sandalwood pulp; อลงฺการ - อะลังการะ — by decorating with ornaments; รกฺษา - รักษา — by chanting protective มนฺตฺรสฺ - มันตรัส; ติลก - ติละกะ — by decorating the body with ติลก - ติละกะ marks in twelve places; อศน - อะศะนะ-อาทิภิห์ - อาทิภิห์ — and by feeding them sumptuously; สํลาลิตห์ - สังลาลิตะห์ — in this way cared for by the mothers; สฺว - สวะ-อาจริไตห์ - อาจะริไตห์ — by their characteristic behavior; ปฺรหรฺษ - ประหัรษะ-ยนฺ - ยัน — making the mothers very much pleased; สายมฺ - สายัม — evening; คตห์ - คะตะห์ — arrived; ยาม - ยามะ-ยเมน - ยะเมนะ — as the time of each activity passed; มาธวห์ - มาธะวะห์ — Lord Kṛṣṇa.

Translation

Thereafter, O Mahārāja Parīkṣit, as required according to the scheduled round of His pastimes, Kṛṣṇa returned in the evening, entered the house of each of the cowherd boys, and engaged exactly like the former boys, thus enlivening their mothers with transcendental pleasure. The mothers took care of the boys by massaging them with oil, bathing them, smearing their bodies with sandalwood pulp, decorating them with ornaments, chanting protective mantras, decorating their bodies with tilaka and giving them food. In this way, the mothers served Kṛṣṇa personally.

คาวห์ - คาวะห์ — the calves; ตตห์ - ตะตะห์ — thereafter; โคษฺฐมฺ - โคษฐัม — to the cow sheds; อุเปตฺย - อุเปตยะ — reaching; สตฺวรมฺ - สัตวะรัม — very soon; หุงฺการ - หุงการะ-โฆไษห์ - โฆไษห์ — by making jubilant mooing sounds; ปริหูต - ปะริหูตะ-สงฺคตานฺ - สังคะตาน — to call the cows; สฺวกานฺ - สวะกาน สฺวกานฺ - สวะกาน — following their respective mothers; วตฺสตรานฺ - วัตสะตะราน — the respective calves; อปายยนฺ - อะปายะยัน — feeding them; มุหุห์ - มุหุห์ — again and again; ลิหนฺตฺยห์ - ลิหันตยะห์ — licking the calves; สฺรวตฺ - สระวัต เอาธสมฺ - เอาธะสัม ปยห์ - ปะยะห์ — abundant milk flowing from their milk bags.

Translation

Thereafter, all the cows entered their different sheds and began mooing loudly, calling for their respective calves. When the calves arrived, the mothers began licking the calves’ bodies again and again and profusely feeding them with the milk flowing from their milk bags.

Purport

All the dealings between the calves and their respective mothers taking care of them were enacted by Kṛṣṇa Himself.

Text 25

Devanagari

गोगोपीनां मातृतास्मिन्नासीत्स्‍नेहर्धिकां विना ।
पुरोवदास्वपि हरेस्तोकता मायया विना ॥ २५ ॥

Text

go-gopīnāṁ mātṛtāsminn
āsīt snehardhikāṁ vinā
purovad āsv api hares
tokatā māyayā vinā
โค-โคปีนำ มาตฺฤตาสฺมินฺนฺ
โค-โคปีนาง มาตฤตาสมินน
อาสีตฺ เสฺนหรฺธิกำ วินา
อาสีต สเนหัรธิกาง วินา

ปุโรวัท อาสว อะปิ หะเรส

Synonyms

go-gopīnām — for both the cows and the gopīs, the elderly cowherd women; mātṛtā — motherly affection; asmin — unto Kṛṣṇa; āsīt — there ordinarily was; sneha — of affection; ṛdhikām — any increase; vinā — without; puraḥ-vat — like before; āsu — there was among the cows and gopīs; api — although; hareḥ — of Kṛṣṇa; tokatā — Kṛṣṇa is my son; māyayā vinā — without māyā.

โค - โค-โคปีนามฺ - โคปีนาม — for both the cows and the โคปีสฺ, - โคปีส, the elderly cowherd women; มาตฺฤตา - มาตฤตา — motherly affection; อสฺมินฺ - อัสมิน — unto Kṛṣṇa; อาสีตฺ - อาสีต — there ordinarily was; เสฺนห - สเนหะ — of affection; ฤธิกามฺ - ฤธิกาม — any increase; วินา - วินา — without; ปุรห์ - ปุระห์-วตฺ - วัต — like before; อาสุ - อาสุ — there was among the cows and โคปีสฺ - โคปีส; อปิ - อะปิ — although; หเรห์ - หะเรห์ — of Kṛṣṇa; โตกตา - โตกะตา — Kṛṣṇa is my son; มายยา - มายะยา วินา - วินา — without มายาฯ - มายาฯ

Translation

Previously, from the very beginning, the gopīs had motherly affection for Kṛṣṇa. Indeed, their affection for Kṛṣṇa exceeded even their affection for their own sons. In displaying their affection, they had thus distinguished between Kṛṣṇa and their sons, but now that distinction disappeared.

Purport

The distinction between one’s own son and another’s son is not unnatural. Many elderly women have motherly affection for the sons of others. They observe distinctions, however, between those other sons and their own. But now the elderly gopīs - โคปีสฺ - โคปีส could not distinguish between their own sons and Kṛṣṇa, for since their own sons had been taken by Brahmā, Kṛṣṇa had expanded as their sons. Therefore, their extra affection for their sons, who were now Kṛṣṇa Himself, was due to bewilderment resembling that of Brahmā. Previously, the mothers of Śrīdāmā, Sudāmā, Subala and Kṛṣṇa’s other friends did not have the same affection for one another’s sons, but now the gopīs - โคปีสฺ - โคปีส treated all the boys as their own. Śukadeva Gosvāmī, therefore, wanted to explain this increment of affection in terms of Kṛṣṇa’s bewilderment of Brahmā, the gopīs, - โคปีสฺ, - โคปีส, the cows and everyone else.

วฺรช - วระชะ-โอกสามฺ - โอกะสาม — of all the inhabitants of Vraja, Vṛndอา - อาvana; สฺว - สวะ-โตเกษุ - โตเกษุ — for their own sons; เสฺนห - สเนหะ-วลฺลี - วัลลี — the creeper of affection; ā-อพฺทมฺ - อัพทัม — for one year; อนุ - อะนุ-อหมฺ - อะหัม — every day; ศไนห์ - ศะไนห์ — gradually; นิห์สีม - นิห์สีมะ — without limit; ววฺฤเธ - วัวฤเธ — increased; ยถา - ยะถา กฺฤษฺเณ - กฤษเณ — exactly accepting Kṛṣṇa as their son; ตุ - ตุ — indeed; อปูรฺว - อะปูรวะ-วตฺ - วัต — as it had not been previously.

Translation

Although the inhabitants of Vrajabhūmi, the cowherd men and cowherd women, previously had more affection for Kṛṣṇa than for their own children, now, for one year, their affection for their own sons continuously increased, for Kṛṣṇa had now become their sons. There was no limit to the increment of their affection for their sons, who were now Kṛṣṇa. Every day they found new inspiration for loving their children as much as they loved Kṛṣṇa.

อิตฺถมฺ - อิตถัม — in this way; อาตฺมา - อาตมา — the Supreme Soul, Kṛṣṇa; อาตฺมนา - อาตมะนา — by Himself; อาตฺมานมฺ - อาตมานัม — Himself again; วตฺส - วัตสะ-ปาล - ปาละ-มิเษณ - มิเษณะ — with the forms of cowherd boys and calves; สห์ - สะห์ — Kṛṣṇa Himself; ปาลยนฺ - ปาละยัน — maintaining; วตฺส - วัตสะ-ปห์ - ปะห์ — tending the calves; วรฺษมฺ - วัรษัม — continuously for one year; จิกฺรีเฑ - จิกรีเฑ — enjoyed the pastimes; วน - วะนะ-โคษฺฐโยห์ - โคษฐะโยห์ — both in Vṛndāvana and in the forest.

Translation

In this way, Lord Śrī Kṛṣṇa, having Himself become the cowherd boys and groups of calves, maintained Himself by Himself. Thus He continued His pastimes, both in Vṛndāvana and in the forest, for one year.

Purport

Everything was Kṛṣṇa. The calves, the cowherd boys and their maintainer Himself were all Kṛṣṇa. In other words, Kṛṣṇa expanded Himself in varieties of calves and cowherd boys and continued His pastimes uninterrupted for one year. As stated in Bhagavad-gītā, - ภควทฺ-คีตา, - ภะคะวัท-คีตา, Kṛṣṇa’s expansion is situated in everyone’s heart as the Supersoul. Similarly, instead of expanding Himself as the Supersoul, He expanded Himself as a portion of calves and cowherd boys for one continuous year.

Translation

One day, five or six nights before the completion of the year, Kṛṣṇa, tending the calves, entered the forest along with Balarāma.

Purport

Up to this time, even Balarāma was captivated by the bewilderment that covered Brahmā. Even Balarāma did not know that all the calves and cowherd boys were expansions of Kṛṣṇa or that He Himself was also an expansion of Kṛṣṇa. This was disclosed to Balarāma just five or six days before the completion of the year.

Text 30

’คาท ธุงกฤไตร อาสรุ-ปะยา ชะเวนะ

Synonyms

dṛṣṭvā — when the cows saw their calves below; atha — thereafter; tat-sneha-vaśaḥ — because of increased love for the calves; asmṛta-ātmā — as if they had forgotten themselves; saḥ — that; go-vrajaḥ — herd of cows; ati-ātma-pa-durga-mārgaḥ — escaping their caretakers because of increased affection for the calves, although the way was very rough and hard; dvi-pāt — pairs of legs together; kakut-grīvaḥ — their humps moving with their necks; udāsya-pucchaḥ — raising their heads and tails; agāt — came; huṅkṛtaiḥ — lowing very loudly; āsru-payāḥ — with milk flowing from the nipples; javena — very forcibly.

ป - ปะli" class="r r-lang-en r-synonyms">

ทฺฤษฺฏฺวา - ทฤษฏวา — when the cows saw their calves below; อถ - อะถะ — thereafter; ตตฺ - ตัต-เสฺนห - สเนหะ-วศห์ - วะศะห์ — because of increased love for the calves; อสฺมฺฤต - อัสมฤตะ-อาตฺมา - อาตมา — as if they had forโค - โคtten themselves; สห์ - สะห์ — that; go-วฺรชห์ - วระชะห์ — herd of cows; อติ - อะติ-อาตฺม - อาตมะ-pa-ทุรฺค - ทุรคะ-มารฺคห์ - มารคะห์ — escaping their caretakers because of increased affection for the calves, although the way was very rough and hard; ทฺวิ - ทวิ-ปาตฺ - ปาต — pairs of legs together; กกุตฺ - กะกุต-คฺรีวห์ - ครีวะห์ — their humps moving with their necks; อุทาสฺย - อุทาสยะ-ปุจฺฉห์ - ปุจฉะห์ — raising their heads and tails; อคาตฺ - อะคาต — came; หุงฺกฺฤไตห์ - หุงกฤไตห์ — lowing very loudly; อาสฺรุ - อาสรุ-ปยาห์ - ปะยาห์ — with milk flowing from the nipples; ชเวน - ชะเวนะ — very forcibly.

Translation

When the cows saw their own calves from the top of Govardhana Hill, they forgot themselves and their caretakers because of increased affection, and although the path was very rough, they ran toward their calves with great anxiety, each running as if with one pair of legs. Their milk bags full and flowing with milk, their heads and tails raised, and their humps moving with their necks, they ran forcefully until they reached their calves to feed them.

Purport

Generally the calves and cows are pastured separately. The elderly men take care of the cows, and the small children see to the calves. This time, however, the cows immediately forgot their position as soon as they saw the calves below Govardhana Hill, and they ran with great force, their tails erect and their front and hind legs joined, until they reached their calves.

The cows had given birth to new calves, but while coming down from Govardhana Hill, the cows, because of increased affection for the older calves, allowed the older calves to drink milk from their milk bags and then began licking the calves’ bodies in anxiety, as if wanting to swallow them.

Translation

The cowherd men, having been unable to check the cows from going to their calves, felt simultaneously ashamed and angry. They crossed the rough road with great difficulty, but when they came down and saw their own sons, they were overwhelmed by great affection.

Purport

Everyone was increasing in affection for Kṛṣṇa. When the cowherd men coming down from the hill saw their own sons, who were no one else than Kṛṣṇa, their affection increased.

Text 33

Devanagari

Synonyms

tat-īkṣaṇa-utprema-rasa-āpluta-āśayāḥ — all the thoughts of the cowherd men merged in the mellow of paternal love, which was aroused by seeing their sons; jāta-anurāgāḥ — experiencing a great longing or attraction; gata-manyavaḥ — their anger disappeared; arbhakān — their young sons; uduhya — lifting; dorbhiḥ — with their arms; parirabhya — embracing; mūrdhani — on the head; ghrāṇaiḥ — by smelling; avāpuḥ — obtained; paramām — the highest; mudam — pleasure; te — those cowherd men.

ตตฺ - ตัต-อีกฺษณ - อีกษะณะ-อุตฺเปฺรม - อุตปเรมะ-รส - ระสะ-อาปฺลุต - อาปลุตะ-อาศยาห์ - อาศะยาห์ — all the thoughts of the cowherd men merged in the mellow of paเต - เตrnal love, which was aroused by seeing their sons; ชาต - ชาตะ-อนุราคาห์ - อะนุราคาห์ — experiencing a great longing or attraction; คต - คะตะ-มนฺยวห์ - มันยะวะห์ — their anger disappeared; อรฺภกานฺ - อัรภะกาน — their young sons; อุทุหฺย - อุทุหยะ — lifting; โทรฺภิห์ - โทรภิห์ — with their arms; ปริรภฺย - ปะริรัภยะ — embracing; มูรฺธนิ - มูรธะนิ — on the head; ฆฺราไณห์ - ฆราไณห์ — by smelling; อวาปุห์ - อะวาปุห์ — obtained; ปรมามฺ - ปะระมาม — the highest; มุทมฺ - มุทัม — pleasure; te — those cowherd men.

Translation

At that time, all the thoughts of the cowherd men merged in the mellow of paternal love, which was aroused by the sight of their sons. Experiencing a great attraction, their anger completely disappearing, they lifted their sons, embraced them in their arms and enjoyed the highest pleasure by smelling their sons’ heads.

Purport

After Brahmā stole the original cowherd boys and calves, Kṛṣṇa expanded Himself to become the boys and calves again. Therefore, because the boys were actually Kṛṣṇa’s expansions, the cowherd men were especially attracted to them. At first the cowherd men, who were on top of the hill, were angry, but because of Kṛṣṇa the boys were extremely attractive, and therefore the cowherd men immediately came down from the hill with special affection.

ตตห์ - ตะตะห์ — thereafter; ปฺรวยสห์ - ประวะยะสะห์ — elderly; โคปาห์ - โคปาห์ — cowherd men; โตก - โตกะ-อาเศฺลษ - อาศเลษะ-สุนิรฺวฺฤตาห์ - สุนิรวฤตาห์ — became overjoyed by embracing their sons; กฺฤจฺฉฺราตฺ - กฤจฉราต — with difficulty; ศไนห์ - ศะไนห์ — gradually; อปคตาห์ - อะปะคะตาห์ — ceased from that embracing and returned to the forest; ตตฺ - ตัต-อนุสฺมฺฤติ - อะนุสมฤติ-อุท - อุทะ-ศฺรวห์ - ศระวะห์ — as they remembered their sons, tears began to roll down from their eyes.

Translation

Thereafter the elderly cowherd men, having obtained great feeling from embracing their sons, gradually and with great difficulty and reluctance ceased embracing them and returned to the forest. But as the men remembered their sons, tears began to roll down from their eyes.

Purport

In the beginning the cowherd men were angry that the cows were being attracted by the calves, but when the men came down from the hill, they themselves were attracted by their sons, and therefore the men embraced them. To embrace one’s son and smell his head are symptoms of affection.

Devanagari

vrajasya rāmaḥ premardher

Synonyms

vrajasya — of the herd of cows; rāmaḥ — Balarāma; prema-ṛdheḥ — because of an increase of affection; vīkṣya — after observing; aut-kaṇṭhyam — attachment; anu-kṣaṇam — constantly; mukta-staneṣu — who had grown up and were no longer drawing milk from their mothers; apatyeṣu — in regard to those calves; api — even; ahetu-vit — not understanding the reason; acintayat — began to consider as follows.

วฺรชสฺย - วระชัสยะ — of the herd of cows; รามห์ - รามะห์ — Balarāma; เปฺรม - ปเรมะ-ฤเธห์ - ฤเธห์ — because of an increase of affection; วีกฺษฺย - วีกษยะ — after observing; เอาตฺ - เอาต-กณฺฐฺยมฺ - กัณฐยัม — attachment; อนุ - อะนุ-กฺษณมฺ - กษะณัม — constantly; มุกฺต - มุกตะ-สฺตเนษุ - สตะเนษุ — who had grown up and were no longer drawing milk from their mothers; อปเตฺยษุ - อะปัตเยษุ — in regard to those calves; อปิ - อะปิ — even; อเหตุ - อะเหตุ-วิตฺ - วิต — not understanding the reason; อจินฺตยตฺ - อะจินตะยัต — began to consider as follows.

Translation

Because of an increase of affection, the cows had constant attachment even to those calves that were grown up and had stopped sucking milk from their mothers. When Baladeva saw this attachment, He was unable to understand the reason for it, and thus He began to consider as follows.

Purport

The cows had younger calves who had started sucking milk from their mothers, and some of the cows had newly given birth, but now, because of love, the cows enthusiastically showed their affection for the older calves, which had left off milking. These calves were grown up, but still the mothers wanted to feed them. Therefore Balarāma was a little surprised, and He wanted to inquire from Kṛṣṇa about the reason for their behavior. The mothers were actually more anxious to feed the older calves, although the new calves were present, because the older calves were expansions of Kṛṣṇa. These surprising events were taking place by the manipulation of yoga-māyā. - โยค-มายาฯ - โยคะ-มายาฯ There are two māyās - มายาสฺ - มายาส working under the direction of Kṛṣṇa — mahā-māyā, - มหา-มายา, - มะหา-มายา, the energy of the material world, and yoga-māyā, - โยค-มายา, - โยคะ-มายา, the energy of the spiritual world. These uncommon events were taking place because of the influence of yoga-māyā. - โยค-มายาฯ - โยคะ-มายาฯ From the very day on which Brahmā stole the calves and boys, yoga-māyā - โยค-มายา - โยคะ-มายา acted in such a way that the residents of Vṛndāvana, including even Lord Balarāma, could not understand how yoga-māyā - โยค-มายา - โยคะ-มายา was working and causing such uncommon things to happen. But as yoga-māyā - โยค-มายา - โยคะ-มายา gradually acted, Balarāma in particular was able to understand what was happening, and therefore He inquired from Kṛṣṇa.

กิมฺ - กิม — what; เอตตฺ - เอตัต — this; อทฺภุตมฺ - อัทภุตัม — wonderful; อิว - อิวะ — just as; วาสุเทเว - วาสุเทเว — in Vāsudeva, Lord Śrī Kṛṣṇa; อขิล - อะขิละ-อาตฺมนิ - อาตมะนิ — the Supersoul of all living entities; วฺรชสฺย - วระชัสยะ — of all the inhabitants of Vraja; ส - สะ-อาตฺมนห์ - อาตมะนะห์ — along with Me; โตเกษุ - โตเกษุ — in these boys; อปูรฺวมฺ - อะปูรวัม — unprecedented; เปฺรม - ปเรมะ — affection; วรฺธเต - วัรธะเต — is increasing.

Translation

What is this wonderful phenomenon? The affection of all the inhabitants of Vraja, including Me, toward these boys and calves is increasing as never before, just like our affection for Lord Kṛṣṇa, the Supersoul of all living entities.

Purport

This increase of affection was not māyā; - มายา; - มายา; rather, because Kṛṣṇa had expanded Himself as everything and because the whole life of everyone in Vṛndāvana was meant for Kṛṣṇa, the cows, because of affection for Kṛṣṇa, had more affection for the older calves than for the new calves, and the men increased in their affection for their sons. Balarāma was astonished to see all the residents of Vṛndāvana so affectionate toward their own children, exactly as they had been for Kṛṣṇa. Similarly, the cows had grown affectionate toward their calves — as much as toward Kṛṣṇa. Balarāma was surprised to see the acts of yoga-māyā. - โยค-มายาฯ - โยคะ-มายาฯ Therefore He inquired from Kṛṣṇa, “What is happening here? What is this mystery?”

Text 37

กา - กา — who; อิยมฺ - อิยัม — this; วา - วา — or; กุตห์ - กุตะห์ — from where; อายาตา - อายาตา — has coเม - เม; ไทวี - ไทวี — whether demigod; วา - วา — or; นารี - นารี — woman; อุต - อุตะ — or; อาสุรี - อาสุรี — demoness; ปฺรายห์ - ปรายะห์ — in most cases; มายา - มายา — illusory energy; อสฺตุ - อัสตุ — she must be; เม - เม — My; ภรฺตุห์ - ภัรตุห์ — of the master, Lord Kṛṣṇa; น - นะ — not; อนฺยา - อันยา — any other; me — My; อปิ - อะปิ — certainly; วิโมหินี - วิโมหินี — bewilderer.

Translation

Who is this mystic power, and where has she come from? Is she a demigod or a demoness? She must be the illusory energy of My master, Lord Kṛṣṇa, for who else can bewilder Me?

Purport

Balarāma was surprised. This extraordinary show of affection, He thought, was something mystical, performed either by the demigods or some wonderful man. Otherwise, how could this wonderful change take place? “This māyā - มายา - มายา might be some rākṣasī-māyā, - รากฺษสี-มายา, - รากษะสี-มายา,” He thought, “but how can rākṣasī-māyā - รากฺษสี-มายา - รากษะสี-มายา have any influence upon Me? This is not possible. Therefore it must be the māyā - มายา - มายา of Kṛṣṇa.” He thus concluded that the mystical change must have been caused by Kṛṣṇa, whom Balarāma considered His worshipable Personality of Godhead. He thought, “It was arranged by Kṛṣṇa, and even I could not check its mystic power.” Thus Balarāma understood that all these boys and calves were only expansions of Kṛṣṇa.

Translation

Thinking in this way, Lord Balarāma was able to see, with the eye of transcendental knowledge, that all these calves and Kṛṣṇa’s friends were expansions of the form of Śrī Kṛṣṇa.

Purport

Every individual is different. There are even differences between twin brothers. Yet when Kṛṣṇa expanded Himself as the boys and calves, each boy and each calf appeared in its own original feature, with the same individual way of acting, the same tendencies, the same color, the same dress, and so on, for Kṛṣṇa manifested Himself with all these differences. This was Kṛṣṇa’s opulence.
